## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: Chemical Kinetics
**Analysis**: This task belongs to chemical reaction kinetics, focusing on how the concentration of a reactant or product changes over time. The rate equation typically exhibits power-law dependence on concentration (reaction order) and may include time-modulated terms representing non-isothermal conditions, catalyst deactivation, or diffusion effects.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order rate: dA_dt = -c0 (constant rate independent of concentration, typical for saturated catalysts)
- First-order rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A (exponential decay of concentration, unimolecular reactions)
- Second-order rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular collision-controlled reactions)
- n-th order rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (general power-law kinetics with arbitrary reaction order)
- Autocatalytic rate: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (reaction catalyzed by its own product, exhibits sigmoidal concentration profile)
- Time-modulated first-order: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A (non-isothermal conditions or time-varying rate constant)
- Fractional-order diffusion-controlled: dA_dt = -c0 * t**c1 * A**c2 (reactions in fractal media or anomalous diffusion environments)
- Self-limiting kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A - c1 * A**2 (finite reactant availability or product inhibition)
- Consecutive reaction step: dA_dt = c0 * exp(c1 * t) - c2 * A (intermediate species formation and subsequent decay)
- Power-law aging effect: dA_dt = -c0 * t**c1 * A (gradual catalyst deactivation or reactor fouling over time)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Integer or fractional concentration powers → Reaction order dependence (dA_dt ∝ A^n)
- Quadratic concentration with sign change → Autocatalysis or reversible equilibrium approach
- Multiplicative time function × concentration → Time-dependent rate constant (temperature ramp or deactivation)
- Non-integer time exponents → Diffusion-limited or fractal kinetic effects
- Linear production minus linear decay → Consecutive series reaction intermediates
- Constant rate until concentration drops → Zero-order surface saturation behavior
- Negative quadratic concentration term → Product inhibition or finite reactant capacity limit

**GT:** `-0.11847*sqrt(A) - 0.11847*A^2 + 0.84638*sin(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three basis functions: `sqrt(A)`, `A^2`, and `sin(log(A+1))`.

Let me analyze each candidate systematically.

### Candidate 1:
`A^(1/3)*c0 + A*c1*(A + c2) + c3 + c4*exp(c5*|c6*log(A*c7 + 1)|)`

This has `A^(1/3)` (not `sqrt(A)`), `A^2 + c2*A` terms, a constant, and `exp(|...|)` (not `sin(log(...))`). The `A^(1/3)` cannot match `sqrt(A)`, and `exp` cannot match `sin`. Setting c0=0 removes the cube root but then we lose `sqrt(A)`.

Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 2:
`A*(A*c0 + c1) + c2*exp(A*c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7)`

= `c0*A^2 + c1*A + c2*exp(c3*A) + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*A + 1) + c7)`

This has `A^2`, `A`, `exp(A*c3)`, and `sin(c5*log(c6*A+1)+c7)`. Missing `sqrt(A)`. We need `sqrt(A)` but have `A` instead. Setting c1=0 removes `A`, setting c2=0 removes `exp`, but we still don't have `sqrt(A)`. Cannot match.

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 3:
`(c0 + (A*c1 + c2)*(sqrt(A)*c3 + A^3*c4 + c5*sin(A*c6 + c7)))/(A*c1 + c2)`

= `c0/(A*c1+c2) + sqrt(A)*c3 + A^3*c4 + c5*sin(A*c6+c7)`

This has `sqrt(A)`, `A^3`, `sin(A*c6+c7)`, and a rational term `c0/(Ac1+c2)`. GT needs `A^2` and `sin(log(A+1))`. `sin(A*c6+c7)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))`. Cannot match.

Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 4:
`sqrt(A)*c0 + A^c1*c2 + c3*exp(A*c4) + c5*sin(A*c6 + c7)`

Has `sqrt(A)`, `A^c1` (can set c1=2 for `A^2`), `exp(A*c4)` (set c3=0), `sin(A*c6+c7)`. But `sin(A*c6+c7)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))`.

Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 5:
`A*c0*(A + c1) + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)`

= `c0*A^2 + c0*c1*A + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(c5*A+1) + c6)`

Has `A^2`, `A`, constant, and `sin(c4*log(c5*A+1)+c6)`. With c4=1, c5=1, c6=0: `sin(log(A+1))`. But missing `sqrt(A)`. The `A` term cannot equal `sqrt(A)`.

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 6:
`A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*Max(0, A-1) + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5+1)+c6)`

Has `Max(0, A-1)` which is piecewise linear, not `sqrt(A)`.

Candidate 6 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 7:
`A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5+1)+c6)`

Same issue as Candidate 5 - has `A` but not `sqrt(A)`.

Candidate 7 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidates 8, 9: Polynomial + exp + log(exp+1). No `sqrt(A)`, no `sin(log(...))`.

Candidate 8 verdict: [NO MATCH]
Candidate 9 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 10:
`(A*c0*(A+c1) + (A+c2)*(A^3*c3+A^2*c4+A*c5+c6))/((A+c1)*(A+c2))`

This is a rational function. GT has `sin(log(A+1))` which is transcendental. Rational functions cannot equal transcendental functions.

Candidate 10 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 11:
Rational function - same reasoning.

### Candidate 13:
`A^2*c0 + A*c1 + c2*exp(A*c3) + c4 + c5*log(c6*exp(A*c7)+1)`

No `sqrt(A)`, no `sin(log(...))`.

Candidate 13 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 14:
`(A^3*c0 + A^2*c1 + A*c2 + c3*(A+c4)*sin(c5*log(A*c6+1)+c7) + c8)/(A+c4)`

= `(A^3*c0 + A^2*c1 + A*c2 + c8)/(A+c4) + c3*sin(c5*log(c6*A+1)+c7)`

The rational part: `(A^3*c0 + A^2*c1 + A*c2 + c8)/(A+c4)`. By polynomial division, this gives `c0*A^2 + (c1-c0*c4)*A + (c2-c4*(c1-c0*c4)) + remainder/(A+c4)`.

GT needs `sqrt(A) + A^2 + sin(log(A+1))`. The rational part gives polynomial + 1/(A+c4), not `sqrt(A)`.

Candidate 14 verdict: [NO MATCH]

`A^3*c0 + A*c1 + c2*log(A*c3+1) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*cos(A*c7))`

No `sqrt(A)`, no `sin(log(...))`.

Candidate 15 verdict: [NO MATCH]

Candidate 19 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 21:
`A*c0*(A+c1) + c2*exp(A*c3) + c4 + c5*sin(c6*exp(A*c7)+c8)`

`sin(exp(...))` ≠ `sin(log(...))`.

Candidate 21 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 22:
`A*(A*c0+c1) + c2*exp(A*c3) + c4 + c5*cos(c6*log(A*c7+1))`

Has `A^2`, `A`, `exp`, `cos(log(...))`. `cos(c6*log(c7*A+1))` = `sin(c6*log(c7*A+1) + π/2)`. With c6=1, c7=1: `cos(log(A+1))`. But GT needs `sin(log(A+1))`, and `cos` ≠ `sin` unless we can add a phase shift. Here we can't add a phase to `cos(c6*log(...))` - it's fixed as cosine. But wait: `cos(x) = sin(x + π/2)`, and if we set c6=-1: `cos(-log(A+1)) = cos(log(A+1))`. Still cosine. We need `sin(log(A+1))` but only have `cos(log(A+1))`. These are linearly independent. Also missing `sqrt(A)`.

Candidate 22 verdict: [NO MATCH]

### Candidate 23:
`(A*c0 + A^c1*c2*(A+c3) + c4*(A+c3)*sin(A*c5+c6) + c7)/(A+c3)`

= `A*c0/(A+c3) + ... ` wait, let me expand:
= `A*c0/(A+c3) + A^c1*c2 + c4*sin(A*c5+c6) + c7/(A+c3)`

Has `A^c1` (set c1=2 → A^2), `sin(A*c5+c6)` ≠ `sin(log(A+1))`, rational terms. Missing `sqrt(A)`.

Candidate 23 verdict: [NO MATCH]
